	martial = 14
	prowess = 14
	trait = blood_of_numenor_4
	trait = lifestyle_blademaster
	trait = education_martial_4
	trait = just
	trait = brave
	trait = diligent
 
	3711.4.3 = {
		birth = yes		
		effect = {
			learn_language = language_sindarin
			learn_language = language_quenya
		}	
	    give_nickname = nick_the_tall
        effect = {
            add_character_flag = {
                flag = had_nickname_event
            }
        }
	}
	
	3795.2.21 = {
		add_spouse = wifeofelendil
	}
	
	4033.7.12 = { # Slain by Sauron in the Last Alliance			
		death = { 		
			death_reason = death_duel	
			killer = lineofsauron
		}
	}
}

#####################
### House Caladir ###
#####################
# Greatest of the houses of Cardolan, House Caladir was established in 2335 by Calatar, a minor noble of Andustar. Falling in love with a local Eriadorim woman 
# in his time in the colonies, he wed her and return to Numenor, but was met with scorn and was basically blocked from the court, derided for his lowly marriage.
# Smarting, Calatar decided to return to the colonies in the future lands of Cardolan. Using his wife's local connections and his own considerable wealth, he 
# built a palatial complex in Argond, and swiftly established himself as the pre-eminent colonial lord of the region which would one day bear his houses name,
# Dol Caladir. 
#
# In time house Caladir became a kingmaker in colonial and then Arnorian politics, their allegiance vital to the control of Cardolan. King Valandil of Arnor's queen, 
# Finduilas, came from house Caladir, and the line would become the Princes of Cardolan after the death of King Tarantor of Cardolan.
